 USB OTG is a tool that can become an important part of your daily life
 jaahir he aapke paas smartphone hoga hi or agar he to memory kii samasya se aap pareshaan to honge hi
 You only see two options - first deal the file or transfer it to the memory card
 lekin ek aisa opshan aapke paas he jise aap primary bana lenge
 If you know about USB OTG then that's good, if you don't know about it, then know today
 is choti divaais ke jariye aap apane smartphone se photose, videos or gane sahit sahit sabhi data ko aasaani se transfar kar sakate hai
 What is USB OTG? USB OTG means USB on the go - this is a standard cable through which the smartphone can be connected to other devices
 aamtaur par aap mobile ko sirf comptuter se conect karte honge, lekin yuasabi otiji se kisi bhi divaais se apane smartphone ko jod sakate hai
 Not only this, you can do many more interesting things through this cable
 iske jariye aap apane smartphone main keyboard, musical instrument yaa storage bhi conect kar sakate hai
 Is USB OTG supported in your smartphone? In the current era, USB OTG is supported in most smartphones
 divaais ke packaging par bhi iske bare main likhaa hota he
 If it is not known on the packaging or you have bought a second-hand smartphone, then you can know about your smartphone on the Internet
 If there is OTG support then it will be recorded in the connectivity feature
 aise karen USB OTG ko profeshnal kii tarah yutub pataa kar liya he ki aapkaa handset otiji ko saport karata he yaa nahin
 Now an OTD cable is required which you can buy on e-commerce or shop
 yah mahaj 60 rupee kii shuruaati keemat ke saath uplabdh he
 You can also connect a keyboard or mouse to a mobile
 Now USB mouse and keyboard are available in the market
 handset main otiji cabel lagaaein or cabel main die gaye port main mouse yaa keyboard ko lagaaein
 Although there is a limit here, it can be used
 iske alaava iske jariye maais conect karke aap cursar yuj kar sakate hai
 When plugged in, you will see the cursor which can be controlled via the mouse
 yah ek alag experience jo aapako shaayad pasand aayega
 Connect the external hard disk directly to the mobile
 Usually you first put the external hard disk in the computer and then store the data of your mobile in it
 yaa hard discs se data mobile main transfer karte hai
 But through OTG cable, you can directly connect external hard disk to mobile, transfer photos, videos and music
 smartphone se conect karen game controlrasmartphone main game khilne ke shaukun hai to kyon ne gempad ko hi isamen jod len
 You can also play games by connecting the Xbox 360's wired controller via USB OTG, just like on a play station or computer

 abhi tak aapane pradhanmantri ko america austrailia or england main rahane vaale apravasi bharatiyon ke bich dekha he, enarai ke rup main bharat main unka dabadabaa bhi rahaa he
 Probably for the first time, this visit of Prime Minister Modi has given importance to millions of Indians who went to work in Arab countries, like nris in America
 sanyukt arab emirate kii aabaadi kaa tees pratishat hissaa bharatiyon kaa he
 More than the local population there have become Indians there
 yahaan azamgarh ke musalmaan rahete hai to siwan ke hindu bhi rahete hai

 ye log har saal 1300 karod rupaya bharat bhejte hai

 khadi deshon main bharat ke sattar lakh log rahete hai

 Both countries condemn such efforts even if they are being done by countries where religion is used to promote or support terrorism against other countries
 
 
 donon desh pashchim or dakshin asia main aise deshon kii koshishon kii ninda karte hai jo raajnneetik muddon or vivaadon ko dharmik or kattar rang dete hai or apane lakshya ko hasil karne ke liye aatankwaad kaa istemaal karte hai

 Here, Prime Minister Modi rode a self-driving car which is powered by a solar charged battery
 is shahar main car main nahin chalati he
 It has a private rapid transport system
 yahaan kii sadakon par self driving kaaren chalati hai
 The city has an area of six square kilometers
 pradhanmantri kii is yatra ko smart city main unki dilchaspee se jod kar dekha ja saktaa he
 In this city, the Prime Minister also held a meeting with the business world and said that there is a possibility of investing three trillion dollars in India
 rail se lekar raksha tak main nivesh kiye ja sakate hai
 In 2013, Mubarak Al Nahyan signed a $ 45 billion investment agreement in Pakistan, the largest ever in Pakistan
 bharat sanyukt arab emirate se baari nivesh kii ummid karata he to uske liye bhi apane aap ko haazir karnaa chahta he
 The shared statements issued by the two countries are also no less interesting
 khadi deshon main bharat ke sattar lakh log rahete hai
 The statement said that the UAE is a vivid example of a multicultural society
 bharti baari vividhta dharmik bahulwaad or mili juli samskruti vaala desh he
 The comments donon desh dharm or aatankwaad ke bich kisi rishte or charampanth ko khaarij karte hai
 
 
 Both countries condemn such efforts even if they are being done by countries where religion is used to promote or support terrorism against other countries
 
 
 donon desh pashchim or dakshin asia main aise deshon kii koshishon kii ninda karte hai jo raajnneetik muddon or vivaadon ko dharmik or kattar rang dete hai or apane lakshya ko hasil karne ke liye aatankwaad kaa istemaal karte hai
 
 
 UAE and India will partner against religious bigotry, it should be discussed rather than why the Prime Minister went to the mosque
 saakshaa bayaan main aatankwaad ko lekar jo baaten kahi gayi wo bhi apane lihaaz se behad ahm hai
 All this will be discussed but first let's go to the stadium in Dubai where fifty sixty thousand people are waiting to hear the Prime Minister
 khadi deshon ke kai hisson se log vahaan sunne ke liye maujuud hai
 Prime Minister Modi repeatedly calls the 21st century the century of Asia
 kya ab vah vakt aa gaya he ki unki is baat ko falsafe ke taur par dekha jaae
 Including this trip, he has traveled to seven Muslim countries
 madhya asia ke daure par media ne kam hi dhyaan diya
 He has gone to Bangladesh before Uzbekistan, Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, Tajikistan and Turkmenistan
 isse pehle ve buddha dharm ke lihaaz se myanmar, korea, srilanka, japan china or mongolia kii yatra kar chuke hai
 If i have counted properly in his foreign trip to 25 countries, then the Prime Minister has visited seventeen big and small countries of Asia
 ravivaar ko jab pradhanmantri shaikh zaayad masjid gaye to isaki aaleeshaan islamic vaastukala par logon kii kam nazar gai
 It is the third major mosque in the world after Mecca Medina which was built in memory of Sheikh Zayed bin Sultan Al Nahyan, the founder of the emirate
 13 saal main bani is masjid main ek saath chalis hazaar log namaaz pard sakate hai
 This mosque is a major tourist attraction
 lekin masjid main modi kii tasviir ko lekar soshal media main unke samarthakon or aalochakon ko ravivaar bhar ke liye acha masala mil gaya
 When some people started calling it a Hindu victory, some people started to ask the same excuse that if they went to mosques outside India and went to the mosques of India, then the Muslims of India would have got a better message
 ye donon hi pratikriyaayein ativaadee or halki hai
 This is mentioned because you cannot ignore this game that is running on social media
 yah hamaari raajnneetik vimarsh kaa bada or mahatvapurn hissaa he
 Why not visit this visit to the Muslim countries of Central Asia again
 nepal ke pashupati nath mandir kii yatra ko hindu chhavi se joda gaya lekin aaj kam hi ko wo chhavi yaad hogi
 The Prime Minister would go to the only gurdwara in Abu Dhabi and his party would do well in Punjab
 videsh yatraaon ko hameshaa is tarah kii sankuchit nazar se nahin dekha janaa chahie
 At least, it should definitely be avoided to make it a spice of Bhakta vs
 Critic's game on Facebook Twitter
 log kitni jaldi bhul gaye ki pradhanmantri ne isi saal ajmer shareef muqataar abbaas naqvi ke haathon chadar bheji thi
 What message did not reach the Indian Muslims or something less that the Prime Minister had to go to this mosque to fulfill
 bijepi ke mahasachiv kailash vijayawargeey ne bhi kah diya ki agar modi ji ke prayaason se abu dhabi main shiv mandir ban saktaa he to ayodhya main bhi bhavy shri ram mandir avashya banegaa
 Just need to be patient until the appropriate time and environment is created
 pradhanmantri modi ne masjid main kaha ki islam shanti sadbhaavna kaa dharm he

 allaah ke baad ilm yani gyaan shabd sabase zyaada baar istamaal hua he
 Which shows what knowledge is important in Islam
 On Sunday, the news of another major decision came which the Prime Minister also described as a milestone
 emirate sarkaar ne bharat ko abu dhabi main mandir banane ke liye zamin dene kaa elaan kiya tha
 There are temples of Lord Shiva and Krishna in Dubai but it is said that there is no temple in Abu Dhabi
 lekin times aaf india kii 2013 kii ek khabar se andeh failaa jisamen kaha gaya he ki kuch musalmaan kaarobaariyon ne gujarat ke swaminarayan sampradaay ko mandir banane ke liye paanch acre zamin di he
 Al Jazeera News website has also written referring to this news that now it is not clear whether the current decision is of the same land or it is a different decision
 vaise google se pataa chalaa ki 2013 ke saal main swaminarayan sanstha ne kai arab mulkon main satsang kaa aayojan kiya tha

 Bharti is a country with enormous diversity, religious pluralism and mixed culture
 tippaniyan Both countries reject any relationship and extremism between religion and terrorism
 
 
 donon desh aisi koshishon kii ninda karte hai chaahe wo deshon dwaara hi kii ja rahi hon jahaan dharm ko duusare deshon ke kilaaf aatankwaad ko badhaava yaa samarthan dene ke liye istemaal kiya jaataa ho
 
 
 The two countries condemn the efforts of countries in West and South Asia that paint political issues and disputes religious and fanatical and use terrorism to achieve their goals
